The Birth of a Beautiful Little Pig 300

— Sakura

Suppose, this is a story about the birth of a beautiful little pig.

The father is young, and likewise, the mother is so young.

The young man, apart from earnestly seeking to improve, has no other extravagant desires. He diligently performs his duties, hoping to gradually rise in position and increase his salary. He is able to maintain a relatively comfortable family life! He is filial to his elders, and he cherishes his wife.

The wife always gives him great comfort and stimulating encouragement. She hopes that one day, her husband will be able to fulfill his wishes and unfurl the blossoms of a great career.

In their happy life, the husband is especially fond of his considerate wife, and the wife, wishing to give her husband an even better, more wonderful image, begins to bear a beautiful fruit!

The beautiful fruit, one time, was plucked from a beautiful tree, and along with it came the beautiful roots, and the beautiful little pig was born into the world!

The grandfather was the first to purse his lips, revealing his most youthful smile! He felt that his life was truly worth living.

Every day he mechanically hugs his unfeeling grandson, opens his mouth, constantly smiling, his whiskers pricking the soft, tender little face. He feels more pleasure and meaning than from puffing on his long pipe for a long time.

He needs his son, for the sake of his own face, to host a grand soup and cake banquet for his grandson, which will naturally bring glory to the family!

A request that is not too demanding, and especially the duty that the newly appointed father, his son, should fulfill.

The days flew by the grandfather’s beard! Tomorrow, the day after tomorrow, the child will be one month old.

The day before, the young father came out from the company, his face as gloomy as the overcast sky after a rain.

The next day, the company's door was plastered with a lawyer's advertisement for a liquidation closure.

He stayed at home all day and did not go out. He told his wife that he had specially taken leave from the company to prepare for the child's one-month-old celebration. The wife was accordingly grateful and happy beyond measure! She even more enthusiastically busied herself preparing this and that, her hands and feet constantly busy.

The maternal grandmother sent a very exquisite, fist-sized golden wooden fish as a gift for her grandson. She made a phone call to let them know that she would take time out to come early the next morning.

The wife happily smiled from the bottom of her heart! But she also blamed her husband for being so inept, how could the wine and dishes not yet be finalized, and the invitation cards not yet sent out early? She said she was willing to invite a few good old classmates to come and see their little angel's little face. She immediately wrote out the invitation cards and asked the maid to deliver them one by one, urging them to definitely honor the appointment and come tomorrow!

After writing the invitation cards, she asked her husband if he needed her to write a few elegant invitation cards for his female friends?

She glanced at her husband with moving eyes, quietly waiting for him to give a very cheerful answer.

But the husband's face was very dejected! Not at all like he was so pleased with himself for hosting the banquet, and she became somewhat unnatural again!

She ran outside for a walk, and when she returned to the house, the husband had run out of the house at some unknown time!

It was not until the evening that she saw him coming home in great haste, his face still as cold as a white plaster cast, so frightening.

She sulkily lay down on the bed and ignored him.

The next day was the actual day of the one-month celebration. Early in the morning, the mother-in-law arrived, first hugging the beautiful grandson and kissing him again and again, her cheeks showing wrinkled chicken skin, and opening her mouth. He asked his daughter why she did not bring the golden wooden fish for the child to let her see it and be happy!

The daughter quickly ran over to open the jewelry box, but immediately cried out (ah)! She hurriedly sternly asked the maid if she had seen the golden wooden fish that Madam had put in the jewelry box for the young master? The maid was so frightened by this question that she felt cold in her heart: Didn't Madam put it in the jewelry box herself?

So she asked her husband again if he had seen it being moved to another place? The husband said that he had not seen the shadow of a golden wooden fish even once.

She was so anxious that she cried, money is not really important, but at least this is an ominous sign, for the child's entire future happiness! She cried so bitterly that the mother did not dare to say much to her. What does it matter if a wooden fish is lost, is it worth acting like that?

Guests arrived one after another, and the wine and dishes had been delivered two hours earlier.

When the guests left after enjoying themselves, the wife could not find her husband. At first, she thought that he was accompanying the guests outside, but later she waited and waited and he did not come back. The people from the restaurant had also left, and when she asked them, they said that they had already received the money! Ah: Then where exactly did he run off to?

The next day, the third day...the husband did not come home!

Disaster Survey 302

— Ya Fei

Although it was late autumn, the weather was still so sultry. The sky was weighed down by a gray-brown cloud, as if a thunderstorm was about to break.

(Today, the county has sent a disaster survey committee to the countryside to survey the damage!) The drunkard A Gen ran over to Yao Jian Sheng, covered in sweat, and reported: (The village head, Wu Datou, told me, and he also asked me to tell you…)

Oh! I understand!) Before he could say anything else, Yao Jian Sheng cut him off, sweeping away the drunkard A Gen's enthusiasm. He himself still squinted his mouse-like eyes, constantly puffing on his long pipe, the pipe squeaking! squeaking! as he did so, watching the gray-white smoke rings he exhaled from his mouth disappear into the air, his expression as if he were planning something.

Yao Jian Sheng was a well-known local notable here. His family owned a pharmacy in this town, and business was very good, so now he had become a small wealthy family. Moreover, because of his skillful tactics, his name was actually quite well-known in the countryside, and even the local officials here had to seek his approval. He did not own any fields, nor was he a tenant farmer, so any disaster had nothing to do with him. However, these district chiefs, village heads, and whatnot, were afraid of him, so whenever anything big or small happened in the village, it seemed that his participation was always essential. The drunkard A Gen was a servant in his house, and today he had made such an effort, only to see his master's cold face, so he dejectedly grumbled and slunk away.

Wu Datou was really busy beyond measure, on the one hand arranging accommodation for the disaster survey committee, and on the other hand going to notify the various local notables. There were also many villagers who wanted to beg him for help, asking him to plead on their behalf before the disaster survey committee, asking him to report the disaster more severely to the county, and to report the percentage of damage more lightly.

The next day, Wu Datou accompanied the disaster survey committee to the countryside to inspect the situation on the ground. District Office Chief Mi, Yao Jian Sheng, and several wealthy and influential gentry were also among those accompanying them. The night before their departure, they had already agreed on a survey procedure, deciding to start from West Bay, return from East Village, and after surveying in this way for a week, they would have a basis when filling out the survey form and reporting to the county.

That disaster survey committee member was short in stature, with a long face, an eagle-like nose, and a Chaplin-style mustache under his nose. He was only around thirty years old, but he was already so old and serious. Although he had an air of authority in front of everyone, he could not hide his addiction to opium. He went to the countryside to investigate the situation on the ground, which was a ghost-driving charade. They sat in seven sedan chairs, going from east to west, from west to east, parading around like a great funeral procession. It was nothing more than putting on a ghost show, who really had the intention of surveying the disaster situation? It was not the sedan chair carriers' legs that suffered the misfortune.

This day was hosted by Yao Jian Sheng, and they had lunch at his house. Several local notables and District Chief Mi were of course guests, and Wu Datou acted as a temporary errand runner.

In the evening, the disaster survey situation was discussed in the district office. In addition to the original crew from the daytime, a district public security chief was added. Originally, according to the disaster survey committee member's proposal, they wanted to report 50% of the damage to the county. However, after everyone's discussion, it was decided to report 40% of the damage to the county, and the disaster survey committee member seemed to agree.

However, the villagers felt that the 40% figure was too unfavorable, and everyone expressed dissatisfaction, but what could they do? They were only dissatisfied in their hearts and dissatisfied in their mouths.

Winter Night Feelings 303

— Rong

Sitting on a circular chair, letting the soft lamplight caress my head, my whole body, and then lazily spilling into the corner of the room, listening to the howling of the wind outside, the low weeping of the rain, a feeling of utter boredom and desolation arises in my heart. Although the stove is burning, my heart is cold,颓唐的, like a pile of burnt incense ashes. At this time, all the past and future events, dressed in very seductive and charming clothes, cling to my side. This taste is also inexplicably mysterious.

Gazing at the dim, bloodless light, I think, only a short time ago, I could see the moon's brightness and the stars' brilliance through the window. The clear autumn sky brought a sense of Longjing tea or green olives, 清涩而又隽永之感. (In an instant, these have all passed quickly, leaving behind only cold, cold, this cold is like a spiral, deeply and sharply rotating into your heart. The艳冶 of spring, the 荣华 of summer, the 秀逸 of autumn, the blooming of flowers, the songs of birds, the sprouting of every plant and tree, the rotation of the sun, moon, and stars, all seem to have nothing to do with winter. What surrounds me is simply a漫漫无尽的 long night, this long night makes me lonely enough to want to cry.

When lonely enough to cry, just remain silent, like the gray sky. Take one or two harmless little books, light a peaceful cigarette, approach the stove, watch the coal gradually消鎔,灰化, watch the flames gradually蕩摇,變幻, it seems that all this before me symbolizes the growth and奄化 of life, say nothing,吐着思想 in your mind,吐着缭绕的 smoke at the corner of your lips, taking advantage of no one's attention, quietly 温理 the past life, this is just like flipping through old books,谛视着前代人的智慧 page by page,剪数着憔悴的 yellow flowers,怀念着消逝了的温馨瓣 by瓣, only in this unforced labor will it bring a深郁的回味, waiting until the stove fire burns out, the灯炧人倦, raise a cup of strong tea to凭吊着 yourself 孤獨的影子,映到墙上的, this can also bring you unspeakable deep comfort.

In my experience, winter nights are the most suitable for silent meditation. No one comes to disturb you, except for the sound of the wind, the sound of the rain, and the sound of the clock that seems to cut up time, and the city sound that is gradually消沉了下去的, because it is cold, you will never think of going out to play, you can only sit at home, because it is cold, you can not officially sit down to do some繁重的工作, or you have no family, or you have family and they are all asleep. Then, I tell you, the most suitable thing for you to do at this time is to quietly do a comfortable fantasy. Every day we are busy,喧嚣,争执,追逐, for food and clothing or for something else in life, thus磨去 us the years that will never return, if there is such an opportunity, allowing you to静下心来, take a真挚的凝视 at life, you silently thinking, silently laughing, as Owen said, this small room is your one person's kingdom, this circle chair is your one person's寶座,随你愤怒,你哀悼,你鼓舞,你歌唱, no one will管你, at this time, your spirit that has not been没世俗的得到茁发与伸长, this life 最自由的一刹那 is simply可说是一刻千金!

After you追忆,感慨,怀念, and all this has passed, the night has slipped away一大段不知不觉中, the sky is black, the people are quiet, then you can easily take off the shackles of the clothes on your body, and use the comfort of sleep to抵償 this day's fatigue.

Li Yanqiu, Legend of the White Snake

Yuan Chang (1120) 11:30 PM to 12:15 AM

Opening (Young Wife Cries for Her Young Husband)

A round bright moon reflects before the window. The beautiful woman inside is not yet asleep. Dressed in mourning white, covered in filial attire. Sparkling tears hang on her red cheeks. She cries, saying that separation in life will eventually have a day of reunion, but how can death allow us to speak together again? My husband has left our child. We, a pair of orphans, are the most pitiable. That mother-in-law treats me so cruelly, using a leather whip to harshly beat me. She says you are a prodigal, ill-fated, and fated to kill your husband, scolding me as a jinx. Then there's that little sister-in-law, stirring things up, her sharp tongue too cunning. Having eaten all kinds of hardships, today, life is like a year. Thinking back to our first meeting at my uncle's house, our affections connected. Thinking back to the engagement, how joyful it was, calling each other brother and sister. Thinking back to holidays and Sundays, going out together, the sweetness of love in the cinema. Thinking back to that wedding night, how we rejoiced, harmonious as fish and water, our hearts intertwined. Thinking back to our honeymoon trip to Suzhou, the beautiful scenery of Tianping and Mudu. Thinking back to the Tangbing celebration, guests congratulating us, the whole family celebrating the joyous occasion. Thinking of last autumn when I was sick, you accompanied me morning and night by the bed. Thinking of the times we playfully joked in the boudoir, the times we meticulously studied academics together. The times we played Western music on the piano together, the times we sang a song and played the strings together. Four years have passed easily, never a quarrel, like ascending to immortality. So it was that we respected each other like honored guests, our love harmonious like zithers. We hoped to grow old together, living a hundred years. Who knew that a thunderbolt would strike from the clear sky, my husband struck down by typhoid fever and entered the Yellow Springs. How pitiful, half of the brocade quilt on the bed is now empty. What joy do I have in this world? My heart breaks into a thousand pieces. I cry out, "Husband!" and call to the heavens. My cries make the heavens sad and the earth miserable, even a heart of stone would shed tears. After crying for a while, she becomes dazed, wondering why the heavens are jealous of beauty. The newly widowed Wenjun finds it hard to endure.

Ms. Wang Bingmei, Tang Poetry

Climbing Orchid Mountain in Autumn, Sent to Zhang the Fifth - Meng Haoran

North Mountain, within white clouds, the recluse is content and joyful. Gazing at each other, trying to ascend to a height.

My heart follows the wild geese as they vanish. Sorrow arises with the approaching dusk; joy is sparked by the clear autumn.

Often I see villagers returning, resting by the ferry on the sandy path. The trees on the horizon are like shepherd's purse;

The sandbanks by the river are like the moon. When shall we bring wine, and get drunk together on the Double Ninth Festival?

Remembering Xin the Great at the South Pavilion on a Summer Day - Meng Haoran

The mountain light suddenly sets in the west, the moon over the pond gradually rises in the east. With loose hair, I enjoy the evening cool,

Opening the window, I lie down in leisure and openness. The lotus breeze carries fragrance, the bamboo dew drips with clear sound.

I want to take up the singing zither and play, but I regret there is no appreciative listener, feeling this, I remember an old friend,

In the middle of the night, I labor in dreams.

Shanghai Shenbao Supplement, Automobile Weekly

1935 American Automobile Production Plan 309

— Yu

丨丨Ford and General Motors Factories丨丨

Major American automobile factories anticipate that automobile demand in 1935 will increase compared to previous years, so they are expanding their production plans for the manufacture of new cars this year to ensure that production and sales are aligned. The New York Auto Show is scheduled to be held in early January. Based on past experience, after the auto show opens, new car sales tend to jump sharply. Consequently, the end of January is the peak sales period for various new cars. However, in reality, the timing of new car launches varies from factory to factory, some in late winter, others in early spring, but the majority occur at the end of the year. When the New York Auto Show is held, all factories simultaneously display their brand-new cars at the show venue for the public to inspect and appreciate. Customers who want to buy cars choose the cars they like from the dazzling and colorful auto show. Therefore, at this time, not only is the factory under great pressure in terms of manufacturing, but also each dealer is vying for customers and showing their strengths to clear a path for their new cars to sell well. This refers to the initial sales competition among car dealers at the beginning of the year. Now, the 1935 production plans of the two major stars among American automobile manufacturers, Ford and General Motors, are described separately below. After reading them, we can understand how optimistic and sweet the automobile dealers view 1935.

We can imagine the enormous scale of Ford's 1935 production plan from their projected figures. Ford plans to manufacture 1,000,000 cars in 1935, worth $415,000,000. This huge number will be sold by 6,000 dealers in the United States. Just in terms of car bodies, those manufactured entirely by Detroit factories will be worth $100,000,000. The steel, iron, and non-ferrous metals required for car manufacturing are worth approximately $75,000,000. In terms of steel alone, in addition to what is produced in Ford's own factories, another $53,600,000 will be spent on purchases from the market. In addition, $6,618,000 will be spent on purchasing malleable cast iron, and $2,683,000 on wrought iron. These are special metal products from the world's largest Rouge River Ford steel and forging factory. The value of wood is $3,000,000.

Rubber is consumed in large quantities in automobile manufacturing, so in 1935, Ford estimates that the tires sold to them by various rubber factories will be worth $22,500,000, and raw rubber $6,000,000. The cost of manufacturing and decorating car bodies is $32,000,000, of which $16,727,000 is used for the needs of cushions, carpets, leather, and decorative items, $11,000,000 for glass, and $4,300,000 for paint.

In terms of manufacturing, Ford has already invested $14,000,000 to expand its steel and power plants. The mechanical equipment in the factories will require another $2,500,000. Ford will pay $74,000,000 in railway transportation fees this year due to transportation needs. The total payroll for Ford's Detroit factory employees will also be $6,861,000. Ford's factories employed 53,000 workers at the end of this summer. Currently, the number has decreased due to changes in the production plan. If the above-mentioned plan is fully implemented, then the estimated number of employees will be 87,000. Former Ford factory workers and machinists in the Detroit area will be hired to work.

General Motors' 1935 production volume is also expected to be very large, but the company's management believes that it is better to distribute the work during the peak production period evenly throughout the year, rather than having a large output at the end of the year, which would cause extreme tension in terms of work. This avoids the unsuitability of both financial and human resources. For this reason, General Motors' 1935 production plan is slightly different from the past. Although they have not formally announced the new car manufacturing plan, it is said that they will first manufacture the Pontiac, then the Chevrolet, and then the Oldsmobile. As for the 1935 Buick, LaSalle, and Cadillac, the public will not know the details until a few months later. We can understand why General Motors wants to predetermine their production plan by reading the following explanation:

According to General Motors executives, the only purpose of adopting the above plan in 1935 is to enable the employed workers to obtain continuous work. The method is to enable the work process in a year to develop evenly, distributing the large amount of work during the peak production period evenly throughout the year. Therefore, the new General Motors car models may not necessarily be seen in early spring, perhaps they will be seen by the public in late summer or early autumn. As for the current situation, General Motors, like other companies, mostly launches all new cars at the end of the year. New cars are rarely seen at other times.

Speaking of the seasonal relationship of car sales, it is also a very interesting and noteworthy matter, because the car market is similar to other markets, with a period of the year when sales are most prosperous, becoming the peak of sales. According to conventional practice, the most popular period for car sales in a year is the first six months of each year, from January to the end of June. The cars sold during this period often account for 60% of the total annual sales. The weakest selling season in a year is the winter months of November and December. At that time, because new cars have not yet been launched, buyers are waiting and hesitant, so the number of transactions only accounts for 7.5%. Sales in April and May account for 24%. From the above figures, we can know that the production situation in the middle of the year is very uncertain. For example, it suddenly expands in the turn of spring and summer, but in the off-season, workers and work must be reduced. This back and forth has both excessive and insufficient phenomena in terms of management and economy. In the busy season, workers have to extend working hours and expand the capacity of work, but in winter, because of sluggish sales, the production volume has to be greatly reduced. The workers' on-again, off-again situation is really very uneconomical, so the General Motors authorities are trying to even out the work, avoiding such tension and slackness, which is very clear.

Rigorous Inspection and Various Features of the Hudson and Terraplane New Cars 310

— Yun

The final road tests and laboratory tests of the 1935 Terraplane and Hudson new cars have now been completely completed. These vehicles will soon be assembled and shipped from the Hudson factory. All the testing work applied to these new cars has been extremely detailed and rigorous. For road driving alone, the total distance has exceeded 500,000 miles. Some of these cars have been traveling on the road, and their mileage has not been less than 100,000 miles. One of the 1935 engines was recently tested with the most rigorous power meter. This type of testing was only applied to aircraft engines in the past, and no car engine has ever been subjected to such rigorous testing.

During the implementation of this power meter test, the engine was driven for as long as nine days under full load. It was driven for 208 hours at a car speed of 76 to 84 miles per hour. As for the crankshaft, it made a total of 50 million revolutions during this test. Each piston traveled approximately 8,000 miles. The spark plugs fired a total of 25 million times. Therefore, using it at the highest gear for a whole year may be roughly equivalent to this test. In this test, the total mileage of the car reached 17,000 miles. Based on the results of this laboratory test and road test, the factory is engaged in the research and improvement of its products, striving for perfection. The performance and robustness of these Terraplane and Hudson new cars are therefore more advanced than before, and their outstanding performance is unparalleled.

One of the features of the new car is the all-steel roof formed by fusion welding. Since the invention of the steel body, this roof has been the dream of body manufacturers. Now, the Hudson factory is uniquely able to solve all the problems and adopt it first. It is truly commendable and valuable. Another feature of the new car is the application of new car management methods. The adoption of new methods has completely cleared the front compartment of the shift lever and handbrake lever. The Hudson Motor Company is currently keeping the details of this new method secret. However, this feature will surely be the most talked about feature of the 1935 new car models by car enthusiasts. This can be asserted.

In terms of appearance, the low, long, and wide body of the new car surpasses the popular styles on the market. As for the excellent and outstanding performance, even the previous styles that have repeatedly created unprecedented records are inferior. This has been proven by various rigorous tests.

The news that the Chrysler Airflow new car is about to be released has been widely spread in the automobile industry in Shanghai. Although the exact situation of the new car is still unknown, it is said that the new transmission and clutch assembled in the new car are unprecedented. Its spaciousness and horsepower are also doubled compared to the past. In addition, what is particularly commendable is that in terms of gasoline consumption, the economic efficiency of the new car is said to exceed the previous year's model by an average of 30%. If this is the case, then it can be asserted that people in the automobile industry in Shanghai are eagerly looking forward to this new car and want to see it as soon as possible.

Current Situation of Charcoal Cars in Hunan Province (Continued) 313

— Yu Qing

Now, summarizing my (Xia Zhengkun's self-proclaimed) personal experience and humble opinions, the application of charcoal in highway transportation is indeed an urgent and vigorously promoted key measure. We all know that charcoal cars are not yet perfect, so they have not been widely adopted. However, for our country that does not produce a drop of gasoline, if we want to talk about national defense and recovering leakage, then even if charcoal cars have some unsatisfactory aspects, we can only temporarily endure them.

Page 26

Generally speaking, charcoal cars in countries such as France, Japan, and Italy can be said to have achieved success. Even in the case of Hunan Province, it has indeed reached the level of application. Therefore, we should not talk about national defense. If we want to talk about national defense, unless we establish a large oil mine, we should spare no effort in all important materials that can replace gasoline, such as charcoal and alcohol. Even the so-called charcoal cars of today are just adding a gas stove. (Except for this, the machinery is still completely gasoline car machinery) In fact, it is because of the limitation of the unremodeled vehicle machinery that unsatisfactory aspects are inevitable. (The biggest dissatisfaction is the lack of power uphill) If we are willing to invest heavily in the remodeling of the entire vehicle, then charcoal cars will be more suitable, which can be expected soon.

Now, taking Hunan Province as an example, the use of charcoal cars (or gas cars) is not yet widespread. Only the provincial government has instructed the Changheng section (Changsha to Hengyang) to be the route for the trial use of charcoal cars. The section is 182 kilometers long, and there are currently 89 charcoal cars running between them. (Used as ordinary long-distance buses) But in reality, there are very few charcoal cars from Changsha to Hengyang. When I and others were in Hunan (end of February 1934), the charcoal cars in the province were only used for transportation in the section from Changsha to Xia Shesi. The mileage of this section is only 57 kilometers. From this, it can be seen that charcoal cars in the province are still in the trial period. Even the engineer Xiang De, who was designated by the province to study charcoal cars, said that these vehicles are mostly experimental in nature. (End)

Shanghai Shenbao Supplement, Film Supplement

Hollywood Astrologer Dariès's Predictions for 1935 (Part 2) 316

— Shu Min

The Hollywood prophet Dariès also has the following predictions for the future of major stars:

Claudette Colbert will encounter a form of violent act, whether unintentional or deliberate, before spring or after autumn this year. She will experience two major changes within the year, but by the end of the year, she will follow Garbo and hide herself away. She will be involved in a scandal this year. If Neil Hamilton wants to film an aviation movie, he will encounter an unexpected disaster. If he hires a stunt double, the stunt double will certainly lose his life or be seriously injured. Kay Francis will be emotionally moved by something this year. She will marry a world-famous star, but the result will be extremely poor, as their personalities are inherently unsuitable for marriage. She will film a movie in Europe, but it will not be successful either.

Maurice Chevalier will marry a dark-haired movie star (referring to Kay Francis), but the result will not be good. He will suffer serious injuries or a broken leg this year. 1935 is the period of Bing Crosby's decline in the film industry. He will soon return to radio, but he will go to England to film a movie. One of his children will become seriously ill, but not fatally. Miriam Hopkins will enjoy great fame this year. Her love life will continue for the next three years, but she will still not marry him. There are rumors that Carole Lombard will reunite with her ex-husband, but this will ultimately not come true. She will marry a man outside the film industry, with a very satisfactory result. She will be hospitalized for several weeks this spring.

Jean Harlow will have great achievements in her career this year, but will not be very happy emotionally. In early spring this year, a film mogul will lose his wife and propose to Jean. But she loves another person, who cannot marry her. As a result, she will marry another movie star, not from MGM. Her marriage will not be happy either. Jean Harlow has no hope of a happy marriage in her lifetime. Gloria Swanson will have unprecedented achievements this year, but she will experience infinite pain in love. Remarriage is possible, but not certain. Adolphe Menjou will become seriously ill between summer and autumn this year. There will also be illness in his family, perhaps his wife, but the family will be harmonious. He will have a son.

Sylvia Sidney will marry this year, but she values ​​her career, so she will continue to work in film after her marriage. By the end of the year, she will suffer from extreme neurasthenia. Mae West's film career will come to an end this year. Afterward, she will focus on writing, producing films, or returning to the stage, resulting in unparalleled success. She will not marry this year, but someone will kidnap or harm her because she has offended people in the lower classes of society. She will have great success on stage in 1936.

Clark Gable will encounter an unexpected disaster this summer. He will be accused by a woman of seducing her daughter. The matter is fabricated, but it will take a lot of unnecessary publicity before the truth comes out. In terms of career, this year will be a year of success for him, but in terms of family, there will be illness. George Raft has reached the highest position in his career. In 1935, he will decline. He wants a divorce but cannot get one, because his wife is firmly opposed to the divorce.

Barbara Stanwyck will file for divorce from her husband this year, but the result will be complete reconciliation, and the couple will be as good as new. She will adopt a red-haired adopted daughter. Loretta Young will have smooth sailing from May this year, enjoying three years of success. She will have great conflicts in her career and love. But she should at least wait until 1936 to get married, because a union before 1936 is unfavorable. After Jeanette Gaynor marries this year, her life will be very happy. But her film career will also come to an end. Shirley Temple will continue to rise this year, but some people want to kidnap her.

Mary Pickford and Douglas Fairbanks's future is very dangerous. There is no possibility for them to restore their marital relationship permanently, but their friendship can still be preserved. Mary will no longer make movies, but will engage in writing and directing. She will have extremely unhappy things happen this year because of a man born in mid-August. Douglas Fairbanks's film career has not developed much. Douglas Fairbanks Jr. will stay in England and marry an actress in England, but the result will not be very happy.

Charles Farrell's acting career will come to an end, and he will work as a director from now on. Ann Harding will have a great film success this year. Jeanette MacDonald will get married this year. She will be deceived, and her jewelry will be stolen by bandits. The remaining predictions are too numerous to mention. Let's wait and see how the above points turn out. (The End)

Film Review

Review of "His Greatest Gamble" 317

— Ling He

His Greatest Gamble

丨 Da Shanghai

A romance story is often very touching. This is a movie adapted from a romantic novel. Thanks to John Robertson's excellent directing skills, it is concretely expressed in pictures, and its touching power is truly profound and moving.

Undoubtedly, the best thing here is the director's technique, especially his handling of mood and atmosphere. He mostly doesn't use music to help the picture, but in the main scenes, the music powerfully enhances the plot (not added music, but the sound effects that should be in the play). The piano sound when Feilipu escapes from prison and visits his daughter at night, such as the gramophone when Feilipu allows his daughter and lover to meet, are all excellent performances. Yes, the director grasps the tone of the play extremely well. From the beginning to the end, he unfolds the bitter taste of life in a quiet atmosphere, and the power of the urgent and agile movements in the rapid rain when Feilipu escapes from prison, such a description, is indeed rare in other films.

Perhaps it can be said that Richard Dix, who played Feilipu, was too rational, not enough to thicken the emotion of the play. Yes, this may not be a loss to this film. But this is ultimately an unrealistic romance. Even if it is said to be very emotional, it will inevitably feel empty to the general audience who demands a realistic expression of the movie.

Review of "Before Midnight" 318

Before Midnight 丨 Nanjing Screening

Covered with a mysterious coat on detective films 丨 such as the recent "Dragon Pool Key" and "Thirteen Women" and the current "Before Midnight", this fact, besides explaining those who escape reality, and many old Chinese novels (when the mountains and rivers are exhausted, the gods come to the rescue) · such absurdities, the only difference is that one side (performs brilliantly on the spot), and the other side first sets up an atmosphere and develops it in a deliberately mysterious way.

Wanting to use so-called mystery to make up for an unintelligible story, this "Before Midnight" is self-defeating, and there are still many unintelligible places. First of all, the relationship between the main characters in the assassination case that serves as the center of this film is not close to the facts. Yes, it is common for people who live a decadent life to change their names because of love or other ugly disputes, but it is too far-fetched to change their names in order to prevent their illegitimate children from knowing their own ugliness, which leads to property disputes and evolves into such a tragedy.

Naturally, after the rich merchant Mr. Ya was killed, the author made the secretary, the secretary's wife, the adopted daughter Qin Qi, the consulting doctor Massey, the waiter Japanese Kuno, the banker Ge Han, whose credit was shaken, and even the maid, all suspected of murder. In terms of relationship and atmosphere, the arrangement is not too bad. In fact, if it can be more precise in structure, why must you use some mysterious ancient clock as a gimmick?

From the perspective of performance, the director Lambert Hillyer is quite attentive. However, due to the shortcomings of the script itself, it finally failed to escape the cliché of ordinary detective films. Among them, the battlefield, which is an important cloud in the development of the plot and also the key to solving the case, such as Fula's wife sneaking into Mr. Ya's bedroom in the dark night, encountering lawyer Smith stealing a woman's diary, Kuno eavesdropping outside the room. Kuno was forced by the detective and was about to reveal the truth, but was suddenly killed by a flying knife, and when the secretary handed the diary to his wife, the detective was hanging outside the window peeking. The producers made great efforts to desperately create an atmosphere of tension and horror, which can certainly grab the audience's attention for a while, but the more sophisticated audience will know that this is just a cliché and old tune in ordinary detective films.

The whole film is darker, with particularly many night scenes. This kind of use of photography techniques such as shadows, dark corners, heavy rain, and lightning to increase doubts and horror is also a (family heirloom) commonly used by detective films.

Among the actors, Ralph Bellamy, who played the detective, performed only adequately, just enough to be strong and healthy, but lacking in intelligence and composure. Claude Gillingwateri, who played the secretary Fula, had a rather good attitude of being a murderer and having nothing to do with it. Retly Blyche's secretary's wife is also very good.

A scene from "Before Midnight," a terrifying blood case that exhausts science, starring Ralph Bellamy 丨 Nanjing Screening

Flying Swallow Society Established 319

The "Leng Yan Society", which has long been famous in North China and praised by the newspapers of Tianjin and Beijing as a revolutionary new force in the Chinese song and dance world, has won praise from various newspapers since arriving in Shanghai, bearing the honor of a pure art organization that is determined to overthrow sensuality. Now, the leader of the society, Mr. Liu, in order to repay the enthusiasm of the support from all walks of life, has specially expanded the internal organization, renamed it "Flying Swallow Society", hired the Nordic dance expert Bratov as a professor, and invited the giant Bao Jun from the literary and artistic world as the opera director. In addition to the full participation of the Leng Yan artists, he has also invited four ladies, He Hui, Na Guan Guang, Mao Li Ying, and Di Chen, from Beijing, who have talent and cultivation in song and dance, to be basic members, who have now arrived in Shanghai. The entire team has been directed by Bao Jun and rehearsing the great opera "Volunteer Army" day and night, and Bratov has been teaching new dance programs to meet the needs of a certain major theater for performance within the month.

Movie Novel

Forsaking All Others (Part 5) 320

— Su Yin

Connie was originally sobbing, but after Dillon entered the bedroom and slammed the door, she stopped crying, and her shoulders stopped moving up and down. She raised her head from her cupped hands and smiled sweetly at Dillon's bedroom, with no tears on her face. She thought, "Might as well go all the way and pretend." So she slowly lay down on the floor, spreading her dress on the ground. She readily knocked over a glass of water on the table, causing the water to flow down from the table. After everything was arranged, she reached out and pulled a table lamp next to her. With a crash, the table lamp fell to the ground. She closed her eyes and lay on the floor, hearing the sound, the bedroom door opened······Dillon ran out and quickly walked to her side. She desperately held back her laughter, gritted her teeth, and straightened her charming corners of her mouth············

The next morning, Herbert and Geoffrey woke up in their hotel room. They felt groggy. Geoffrey soon woke up. He suddenly remembered the bachelor's dinner party last night. He also remembered that Dillon had not attended. He jumped out of bed in a flash. At this time, the manager and deputy manager of the hotel were knocking on their door to negotiate with them because they had opened the water pipe in the bathroom all night, and the flood had flowed down, damaging two floors, and they had to pay for the loss.

Geoffrey thought he couldn't manage so many things. He had things to do that were bigger than the sky. Mary was getting married this afternoon, and it was already eleven o'clock. He got out of bed and immediately went to the phone to call the phone number of a flower shop. This was when Herbert was still lying in bed, half-awake, with his eyes half-open and half-closed, asking, "What are you doing?" Geoffrey said, "From the time we were little, Mary loved cornflowers the most. Today is her wedding day, and I should at least send her some cornflowers. I'll buy all the cornflowers they have and send them to Mary······".

In the afternoon, the flower shop sent many, many cornflowers to Mary's house. In her dressing room, many bridesmaids and Paula were busy around Mary. Mary smiled at the many cornflowers and said, "Dillon has a good heart and sent so many cornflowers. When I was little, I liked to sleep in cornflowers······I once said that I would wear a cornflower dress when I got married. Fortunately, Dillon has a good memory, he still remembers it."

That's right, Dillon has a good memory. He remembers everything, except one thing, he forgot to go to the church. Relatives and friends have arrived. The seats in the church were full. The choir on the stage sang for a long time, and their throats were about to sing hoarse. Everyone stretched their necks and waited for the groom to come, but the groom didn't know where he had gone. The guests gradually felt surprised and uneasy. Geoffrey ran out and went to Dillon's apartment to see what was going on. Soon, he came back. Mary greeted him with a bitter smile. Geoffrey's face was ashen. He almost didn't know what to do. He almost couldn't speak. He grabbed Mary's arm and said, "Mary······I······".

Mary knew that something was wrong, and her face changed in fright. She quickly asked, "What's wrong? Is he sick······He······" Geoffrey said, "Mary······he's already married······" Mary followed suit, "Married?" Paula interjected, "Who did he marry?" Herbert said, "Connie Barnes!" Everyone then looked at Mary. She reluctantly asked Geoffrey, "You're not kidding me, are you? Tell me the truth······Don't tease me······". (To be continued)
